In 2015 persons handling special mineral oils submitted 630 notifications.
Providing and failing of special mineral oils or means of transport, the tax administrator must express the tax manager when he finds the handling of special mineral oils without registration or when the registered person fails to comply with his notification requirement.
As in the case of failure to comply with the transport of excise goods, these deficiencies cannot be remedied additionally.
Registration of a fuel distributor is mandatory for persons who sell or are entitled to sell fuel.
Registered fuel distributors can only be persons meeting the following criteria:
Compulsory concession of the business office (specific form of business permissions).
The application for a concession or, where appropriate, to the provision of a responsible representative, shall be given an opinion by the customs office examining whether the applicant for a concession, the statutory body or members of the statutory body of the applicant - the legal person and the designated responsible representative meet the condition of reliability.
If these persons fulfil the condition of reliability, the customs office shall give an approved opinion.
A reliable person is a person of integrity, in terms of criminal property, customs and tax law.
The condition of issuing the concession is professional competence.
The absence of the same circle of persons as in the case of reliability.
A debt-free person is a person who provides sufficient guarantees that he will perform his payment duties to the state in a proper and timely manner, i.e. has no arrears to the state budget and general health insurance.
The fuel distributor must not be prohibited by a court or administrative authority by a court or an administrative authority to prohibit the activity of his or her activity.
The fuel distributor must not be liquidated or bankrupt.
Bail composition (bank guarantees, if applicable) of CZK 20 (i.e. Approx. 740 €) which can be reduced to CZK 10 after three years of registration of a fuel distributor and other conditions after three years of registration and fulfilment of other conditions to CZK 000 (i.e. Approx. 370 000).
Notice of fuel distribution is required by the distributor to the customs office within 20 days after the end of the calendar month.
The electronic notification must contain data on individual purchase and sale of fuel.
The notified data are data on business partners, documents numbers, selected product, quantity, price, carriers and transport, place of loading and unloading.
The right to refund the tax on mineral oils consumed in primary agricultural production was reintroduced at the end of 2014.
Return of excise duty on mineral oils can only be claimed in the case of activity that is apparently related to the land activity.
In 2015 it was about 64 thousand. tax refund claims totaling 1 172 844 CZK (i.e. 43 720 401 €).
Since 2017, the government of the Czech Republic introduced a refund of excise duty on fuel to farmers with animal production.
Farmers or breeders who are dealing with bovine, pigs, poultry, sheep and goats will newly be able to claim this claim.
Tobacco products
Reduction of sales of tobacco products with old tax rate
The Czech Republic has introduced restrictions on the sale of tobacco products with effect from 1. 1. 12. 2014 tobacco products with an old tax rate in case of change in the tax rate.
The excise duty on tobacco products is paid by using tobacco stickers.
The use of a tobacco sticker means placing it on a unit package (Section 116 of the Excise Tax Act).
For the use of the excise duty rate, the production of a tobacco product in a state intended for the final consumer is determined, without removing, supplying, dispatching or selling to the final consumer.
The letter of the alphabet characterizing the excise duty rate is stated on the tobacco sticker together with the price for the final cigarette consumer, the label also indicates the number of pieces in the package or. amount of tobacco smoking in kilograms.
Tobacco sticker has no identifier.
The length of the transitional period for the sale of unit packs of cigarettes intended for direct consumption and bearing a tobacco label with the previous (old) tax rate was fixed until the end of the last day of the second calendar month after the effectiveness of the new excise duty rate.
The development of tobacco stickers in 2014 and the comparison with the previous years shows that manufacturers of tobacco products significantly frontloaded tobacco products with an ′′ old ′′ tax rate, thus reducing the effectiveness of the ′′ new ′′ tax rate by about one year.
Raw tobacco tax
Due to the abuse of raw tobacco to produce tobacco products without the permission of the tax administrator and non-taxation, a tax on raw tobacco and monitoring the handling of raw tobacco was introduced as a measure against tax fraud.
Effective from 1. 7. 2015 excise duty is subject to raw tobacco not used or delivered for the manufacture of tobacco products to another Member State or third country or for which origin, purpose of use or person to whom it was not proven or raw tobacco should be supplied.
Restrictions on handling raw tobacco
Measures such as the supervision of transport and production of tobacco products, marking of unit packaging with control tape and sales restrictions at defined locations were added to the restrictions on the handling of raw tobacco.
Production equipment for processing tobacco raw materials and production of tobacco supervisory products by the customs authorities is not subject.
Only a registered person can store raw tobacco for a purpose other than the manufacture of tobacco products, but such tobacco must not be further processed or modified.
The registered person can only be a person fulfilling the personal conditions of the applicant, the statutory authority and the responsible representative, which is valid throughout the period of registration.
The conditions of registration are: (a) authorization to operate a business allowing the activity of a person storing raw tobacco, (b) reliability, (c) debtlessness, (d) the fact that a person stored raw tobacco has not been prohibited from carrying out an activity preventing the activity of his / her activity; (e) the fact that the person stored raw tobacco is not in liquidation or bankruptcy, (f) granting bail of CZK 20 000 (i.e. Approx. 740 000).
Electronic registration must contain the date of receipt or dispensing of raw tobacco, document number, business partner identification, quantity and type of raw tobacco.
Notice of any acquisition of raw tobacco by a registered person storing raw tobacco must be made between 24 and 72 hours before receiving or dispatch.
Business partner data, raw tobacco quantity, storage address, purpose of use and carrier data are reported.
Notice of the expected quantity in the relevant year of raw tobacco received or dispatched raw tobacco shall be submitted by the body together with the registration application or by the end of January of the relevant calendar year.
Notifications are submitted via an electronic data box in PDFa format.
The transport of raw tobacco must be accompanied by a document with the prescribed elements.
Excise tax legislation in SR
The legal framework regulating excise duty area in SR is based on EU legislation, thus co-creating its uniform tax system.
Individual types of excise duties are taxatively determined by the legislation of the SR, which is similar to the legislation of surrounding countries.
Definition of legislation in SR
Legislative adjustment of excise duties is ensured by four laws according to individual subjects of taxation.
Harmonization was achieved by passing the following excise duty laws: Act No. 98/2004 Z. z., on excise duty on mineral oils, law no. 106/2004 Z. z., on excise duty on tobacco products, law no. 530/2011 Z. z., on excise duty on alcoholic beverages, law no. 609/2007 Z. z., about excise duty on electricity, coal and natural gas.
All excise duty laws constitute statutes of material law and deal with taxation of the subject matter in tax territory.
Act No. 563/2009 Z. z., about tax administration (tax order), is a regulation of procedural law, regulates tax management, rights and obligations of tax entities and other persons.
This legal framework transposed the various provisions of Council Directive 2008/118 / EC of 16. December 2008 on general excise duties and repealing Directive 92/12 / EEC and transposed by it as well as the provisions of other directives and legislation European Community.
Structure of amendments to legislation for individual types of excise duties in relation to the subject matter of control in SR
Since 2011, legislation on the management of excise duties has undergone several major changes according to the structure of individual excise duties.
In the EMCS system, monitoring of the transport of selected excise products under excise duty suspension regime was changed from a documentary accompanying administrative document to an exclusively electronic system where these transports are monitored in real time.
Under the EMCS electronic system, the institute of suspending access to tax entities was introduced in 2015
This segmentISintentionallyLEFTblank
The customs office has the opportunity to suspend access just because of a reasoned fear of the outstanding or undetermined tax on previous taxation periods and its unenforceability.
This applies to the maturity of the tax because the transport of excise goods requires the composition of collateral, which is released by termination of transport.
Excise duty on mineral oils
A fundamental change in the management of the excise duty on mineral oils occurred in 2011, when the option of using the so-called was cancelled. red diesel.
The marked gas oil, commonly called red diesel, was one of the mineral oils.
In the past red diesel has been used for specific law-defined purposes, e.g. in agriculture and its use was favoured by lower excise duty rate.
This change had a positive impact on the income part of the state budget.
The aim of repealing red diesel was to reduce the government deficit, simplify the system of taxation of mineral oils and reduce the administrative burden of the business entities concerned.
In 2012 a new type of tax entity was created, namely the fuel seller.
The purpose of this statutory amendment was to introduce a registration obligation for all gas stations.
Clarity of movement of taxed petrol and diesel is bound to the obligation to buy petrol and diesel from the fuel distributor.
New institutes of fiscal entities were introduced in 2014, namely the distributor of fuels and fuel consumer.
This change contributed to the elimination of tax evasion in petrol and diesel and cleared the movement of these propulsion agents (see Annex No. 4, scheme A).
As part of the fight against tax evasion, lawful provisions on the registration of tax operators dealing with lubrication and essential oils have been extended.
However, in SR these mineral oils are not subject to an indication obligation.
Excise duty on tobacco products
In the fight against tax evasion and monitoring tobacco raw material, the scope of the tobacco law has been expanded and a new tax entity - a tobacco trader was introduced.
Tobacco raw material is not a harmonized tobacco product and its movement is not monitored within the EU.
The obligation to register technological equipment for the production of tobacco products was also introduced.
Legislative brought a new system of ordering, assessment, printing, distribution and use of control signs intended for the labelling of tobacco products.
The check mark is for cigarettes, cigars, cigarillos and tobacco.
Under the new system, the customer of the control stamps must request the customs office to issue inspection marks electronically, via the information system for inspection signs.
This step introduced electronic communication between the tax operator and the tax manager.
One state printer of control signs was established - in Kremnice Mint.
The exercise of tax supervision of the print of inspection signs was also introduced.
Changes have contributed significantly to eliminating tax evasion.
The new system of printing control signs strengthens the system of goods control, because the control mark generates a unique identification number, which can simply be verified whether the goods originate from legal sources.
Unique 8. digit identification number (1.- 2. place is the check sum; 3. place determines whether the code belongs to a check mark or a pack of packages; 4. place is the identifier of the series; 5.- 8. the place is an alphanumeric part of the sequence; 9.- 12. place is a decimal part of the sequence) can also be applied in the form of two dimensional barcode.
The control mark intended for the labelling of cigarettes must further indicate the price of cigarettes, the sign for the validity of the excise duty rate, the number of cigarettes in the packaging and the length of cigarettes.
Excise tax on alcoholic beverages
The biggest legislative change touched alcohol, wine and beer, because the original three materials were abolished and one common law on excise duty on alcoholic beverages.
The law was developed mainly due to the need for a comprehensive solution to the issue of taxation of alcoholic drinks, solutions to their production, movement monitoring, tax provision, as well as the need to improve the business environment in the area, streamline tax administration, reduce administrative burden on small and medium-sized entrepreneurs.
A new way of addressing the issue of taxation of individual types of alcoholic beverages introduced the application of a uniform excise duty rate on an alcoholic drink and took into account the volume percentage of the actual alcohol content.
For non-sparkling wine, sparkling wine and fermented drinks, the volume percentage of the actual alcohol content of the final product is taken into account.
The concentration of beer is also expressed in volume percentages of the actual alcoholic strength of the finished product.
A category of small producer of fermented drinks has been introduced, the essence of exemption from excise duty for a natural person who produces a sparkling fermented drink for their own consumption and for the consumption of their household not exceeding 1 liters per marketing year.
Legislative brought a new system of ordering, assessment, printing, distribution and use of control signs intended for the labelling of the alcohol consumer packaging.
Under the new system, the customer of the control stamps must request the customs office to issue inspection marks electronically, via the information system for inspection signs.
This step introduced electronic communication between the tax operator and the tax manager.
One state printer of control signs was established - in Kremnice Mint.
The exercise of tax supervision of the print of inspection signs was also introduced.
Changes have contributed significantly to the elimination of tax evasion (see Annex No. 4, Scheme B) and elimination of falsification of control signs.
The new system of printing control signs strengthens the system of goods control, because the control mark generates a unique identification number, which can simply be verified whether the goods originate from legal sources.
Unique 8. digit identification number (1.- 2. place is the check sum; 3. place determines whether the code belongs to a check mark or a pack of packages; 4. place is the identifier of the series; 5.- 8. the place is an alphanumeric part of the sequence; 9.- 12. place is a decimal part of the sequence) can also be applied in the form of two dimensional barcode.
Comparison and evaluation
Comparison
Excise taxes on alcohol, mineral oils, tobacco products, beers, wines and intermediates are regulated by one common law in the Czech Republic. 353/2003 Coll.
Solid fuel tax, natural gas tax and some other gases and electricity tax are part of Act No. 261/2007 Coll.
In contrast, in SR, every excise duty is regulated by a special law, except for the excise duty on alcoholic beverages, beer, wine and intermediate products.
Special law regulates excise duty on electricity, coal and natural gas.
In the Czech Republic, since 1. June 1., the issuance of an authorization for the handling of excise products under the excise duty law is conditional, among other things, on the basis of the evidence of the economic stability of the applicants, which the customs authorities verify annually by carrying out a financial analysis.
In SR, a similar form of analysis is carried out only when deciding to abandon or reduce tax security.
FG SR exercises tax supervision in the form of a staff member of the Financial Directorate over the handling of inspection signs for alcohol and tobacco products, their disposal in the printer and their sales to individual customers.
The law provides that the state company Mint Kremnica secures the production of control signs.
The production of tobacco stickers and control bands in the Czech Republic is not introduced in the printer.
Tobacco stickers and control tapes will be taken over from the printer by the designated territorial workplace of the customs office in Kutná Hora.
Tobacco stickers are taken over by their customers at this territorial workplace, control bands for alcohol marking are distributed to individual local tax administrators according to the point of marking.
The legislation of the Czech Republic does not define the manufacturer of tobacco stickers and control bands.
In SR there is an obligation to register technological equipment for the manufacture of tobacco products or parts thereof, such an obligation is not introduced in the Czech Republic.
In the Czech Republic, the tobacco sticker carries excise duty on tobacco products, paid when collecting tobacco stickers at the designated customs office.
On the other hand, the SRR does not contain excise duty on tobacco products.
In the Czech Republic, the refund of excise duty on mineral oils was introduced during the controlled period, in case of their use for primary agricultural plant production, so-called. green diesel.
Since 2017, this tax refund has been extended to animal production.
Such support for farmers is not introduced in SR (existed until 12. 31. 2010 as the so-called. red diesel).
In order to strengthen the fight against tax fraud, a bail of 20 miles was introduced for fuel distributors in the Czech Republic. CZK (i.e. 740 thousand. €).
As a result of the introduction of this measure, the number of fuel distributors decreased from 1 891 entities in 2013 to 174 in 2014 (i.e. decrease by 1 717 tax entities).
In SR, a similar institute of a fuel distributor is introduced, but without making the bail needed to secure the excise duty on mineral oils.
303 distributors registered in SR in 2014 and 407 distributors registered in 2015
The Institute of Fuel Vendor and Fuel Consumer is introduced in SR, which is issued by the local competent customs office.
There is no such institute in the Czech Republic.
In the Czech Republic, selected mineral oils and some other mineral oils are subject to markings, in SR after the cancellation of the so-called. red diesel labelling of mineral oils is not applied.
In the Czech Republic, the alcohol marking control tape contains an eight-digit individual code used to verify the origin of alcohol and a-digit registration code, indicating the spirit drink, according to which the control belt registration is kept.
The destruction, loss and return of the control tape shall be registered on the following working day.
The belt holder is obliged to notify their use within the same period.
In the SR, the control mark intended for the marking of alcohol in the consumer packaging contains a unique-digit identification number, which is communicated once a month to the tax administrator and serves to verify the authenticity of the check mark.
The registration contains the number of checks collected, used and relics.
The Czech Republic and the SR instituted compulsory registrations, or. alcohol distributor's registration.
In SR, registration is subject to compliance with conditions bound, inter alia, to a storage area exceeding 200 m2; annual turnover from the sale of a consumer packaging alcohol at least 100 000 or paid basic property of at least 100 €; minimum number 10 employees.
In the Czech Republic, the acquisition of registration is conditional, among other things, on the basis of a deposit of CZK 5 000 (i.e. 185 000) for the benefit of the tax administrator for the entire period of validity of registration.
This segmentISintentionallyLEFTblank
In SR, the permanent presence of the tax administrator is required in the production of alcohol not only in the consumer packaging.
In the Czech Republic, a special form of registration of a person compulsory to sign alcohol with the condition of the deposit for the benefit of the tax administrator from 100 000 CZK (i.e. 3 700) up to 000 5 (i.e. 185 000) according to the quantity of control bands collected and installation of a tracking device with continuous access by the tax manager.
Evaluation
The legislation of the Czech Republic and the SR exceeds the EU minimum requirements for the subject matter and management of excise duties and responds to identified risks from other Member States and to the risks identified in tax areas.
Legislative changes adopted during the controlled period allow tax administrators to prevent possible tax evasion from developing.
In the Czech Republic and SR to combat tax evasion in the form of abuse of tobacco raw material (e.g. leaves) an excise duty on raw tobacco or raw tobacco has been introduced beyond EU legislation. tobacco materials.
Although raw tobacco and tobacco are not a harmonized tobacco product, the Czech Republic and SR monitor their movement.
NKÚ Czech Republic and NKÚ SR can recommend that this measure be applied in other EU Member States.
Good practice in the Czech Republic demonstrated that the examination of economic stability in applicants for authorization under the Excise Tax Act has been successful because it reduces the risks of tax arrears.
For this reason both control institutions recommend applying such verification also in the conditions of the SR.
Distribution of control stamps is more effective in SR than in the Czech Republic, because it does not burden customs authorities with costs related to transport between printer and customer of control bands and tobacco stickers.
The financial management of the SR has a better overview of the existence and location of technological equipment for the production of tobacco products.
However, the collection of tobacco products tax is more effective in the Czech Republic, because the order of tobacco stickers itself is a tax return with subsequent tax payment.
The financial management in the SR has improved overview of the places of fuel sales due to the introduction of the institutes of ' fuel seller ' and ' fuel consumer '.
The introduction of compulsory marking of mineral oils in the Czech Republic makes it easier to control the abuse of mineral oils with a reduced tax rate or. tax exempt.
A new control tape was introduced in the Czech Republic (2013) and in SR (2014). a sign containing an identification code.
The control tape in the Czech Republic also contains a registration code, while in the SR the new legislation has dropped its introduction.
Impacts cannot yet be evaluated due to the short effectiveness of legislative changes.
The introduction of effective labelling of the consumer packaging of alcohol by a control mark or the tape is an effective measure to combat tax evasion.
NKÚ SR and NKÚ Czech Republic can recommend the introduction of this control measure in other Member States.
SR's attitude towards the conditions for distribution of alcohol characterizes a proclient approach that does not block tax entities funds.
On the other hand, the Czech Republic's approach is rather restrictive because it introduces bail burden on tax entities cash flow, but reduces the risk of tax arrears more.
Development of excise tax revenue
Excise tax is an indirect tax imposed by the state to increase state budget revenue and also regulate the quantity of goods sold, which is considered harmful to individuals and / or to the company (tax regulatory function).
According to the Commission Communication: EUROPE 2020-Strategy for smart and sustainable growth promoting inclusion of 3. 3. under the flagship initiative Europe less resource demanding is the European Commission's intention to improve the framework for using market-based instruments, MJ. in the form of a revision of energy taxation focusing on reducing energy and resources consumption.
In order to fulfil the EK's intention, Member States should try to shift tax burden from the workforce, among other things, to energy and ecological taxation.
The collection of tax revenue from excise taxes in the Czech Republic and SR includes excise duties on mineral oils, tobacco products, alcohol, beer, wines and intermediate products, natural gas, solid fuels and electricity.
The share of excise taxes in total tax revenue and the share of GDP is monitored, inter alia. Organization for Economic Cooperation and Development (OECD).
The two top control institutions used the following selection criteria to enter the query on the OECD website.
Excise tax collection in connection with macroeconomic indicators in the Czech Republic
In the Czech Republic, the share of excise taxes in total tax revenue and the share of GDP according to OECD data decreased slightly.
The European Central Bank's course of the ECB was used to convert the amounts in CZK to € 12. 31. of the relevant year.
The nominal course of CZK vis-).-vis).-vis).-vis).-vis).-vis).-vis).-vis).-vis).-vis 2013
The reason was mainly the monetary policy decision of the CNB banking council of 7. November 20136.
Results of excise tax debit, excise duty rates and per capita income in € decreased significantly due to the exchange rate difference.
A significant reduction in the 2014 excise duty share was caused by a one-time outage of excise duty income on tobacco products due to the impact of the new legislation limiting the sale of old tax tobacco products.
The share of excise taxes is also influenced by the increase in income tax recovery, which has increased significantly due to the improved overall economic situation of the Czech Republic.
The total excise duty collection has the largest share of excise duty on mineral oils (about 55,7 % in 2015) but despite significant growth of the economy against 2012, it fell.
The debit of excise duty on mineral oils in 2013 and 2014 was significantly lower than in 2012 and 2015, although registration of fuel distributors was introduced as a measure against tax fraud.
The trend of ecologically economical vehicles and biofuels is negatively reflected in the tax revenue.
A negligible share of natural gas tax, solid fuel tax and electricity tax, which is caused by a low tax rate compared to the surrounding countries, which is close to the minimum rates established by the EU.
If there is no increase in tariffs, their share will in the future with regard to the ever-decreasing energy performance of buildings and production processes.
The collection of excise duty on alcohol in 2013 and 2014 was negatively affected by the reverberation of a large case of tax fraud consisting of putting taxless alcohol, alcohol containing methanol or insufficiently denatured alcohol into circulation in the form of spirit drinks.
In 2015, after taking a series of measures against such action and after reviving the liquor market, excise duty excise duty on alcohol exceeded 4 miles. €.
The share of tobacco product tax increased due to increasing rates.
The basic excise duty rates changed between 2012-2015 for the tobacco product tax, where the rate increased mainly due to the compliance of Council Directive 2011/64 / EU, on the structure and rates of excise duty on tobacco products.
Due to the currency intervention of CNB, the real rate of excise duty in €, apart from tobacco product tax, has dropped significantly. For tobacco products, it has risen slightly.
In relation to price growth, GDP or standard of living, the indexation of the excise duty rate is not set, so the function of excise duties consisting of regulation of socially problematic activities does not have to be fulfilled.
With the economic growth of the Czech Republic and the growth of living standards, real excise tax rates are decreasing.
7 Indexation - automatic adjustment of a certain economic quantity about inflation, this adjustment is based on a law or contract (for pensions paid by the state is called ad valorization).
Excise tax collection in connection with macroeconomic indicators in SR
In the current legislation of excise duties in SR, the indexation of the amount of excise duty rates is not solved on the evolution of consumer prices, because they are fixed.

Of all excise duties introduced in Slovakia, the largest share of the year-round tax revenue of the state budget has excise duty on mineral oils, with its share not falling below 52 % throughout the controlled period.
The second largest share is the excise duty on tobacco products.
On average, this tax accounts for around 32 % of the total excise tax collection.
Between 2012 and 2015 there was a growth in excise duty per capita of SR.
This development is due to an increase in the rates of excise taxes on tobacco products, higher acquisitions and higher population consumption in a given year.
The growth of excise tax debit per SR is constant and corresponds to the development of excise duty rates on tobacco products, higher purchasing capacity and higher consumption of the population in a given year.
In the Czech Republic, the reduction in income in € per capita is affected by CNB intervention in the currency rate of the crown against the euro.
The difference between the Czech Republic and SR in the total collection from the SPD is due mainly to the collection of excise duty on mineral oils and tobacco products, which is about 2,7 times in the Czech Republic or. 2,8 times higher, however, per one inhabitant of the Czech Republic is only about 1/3. higher for these selected products.
The cause is the lower price of these selected products in the Czech Republic due to lower excise rates in the Czech Republic and the CZK course against vůči for foreign consumers.
For mineral oil tax, the cause is also greater transit through the Czech Republic and cross-border purchases.
In the case of tax on tobacco products, growing foreign tourism to the Czech Republic and cross-border purchases have a negligible influence.
The evaluation of the real rate of excise duty in the Czech Republic due to CNB interventions decreased.
The share of energy taxes in the Czech Republic and SR in total tax revenue does not rise and there is no diverting from taxation of work to taxation of consumption of selected products subject to excise duties, which is not in line with EU strategies.
However, the amount of excise duty achieved is permanently above average compared to the OECD average.
The total excise tax debit is mainly influenced by changes in excise duty rates, economic condition and the behavior of the population.
Future excise tax recovery outages due to environmental measures subsidized by the state in various forms will need to be replaced by other revenue or reducing state spending.
The fact that the indexation of excise duty rates is not introduced in the Czech Republic and SR, their regulatory functions decrease and the EU's aims of less dependent on ecologically unfriendly resources and reducing alcohol and tobacco addiction.
The higher excise duty per capita in the Czech Republic shows higher consumption of selected products by foreign consumers, which is affected by the lower total price of selected products in €.
Administrative expenses of excise duties
The effectiveness of administrative costs reflects the relationship between spending and income related to the management of excise duties, i.e. Expresses the amount of expenditure for 100 units of revenue (CZK, €).
The higher the resulting value, the worse the effectiveness of administrative costs is.
The effectiveness of the tax manager in tax management affects the competence and organisational arrangement of the tax manager, management of the organization, the legal environment and the level of electronization of individual activities.
Determination of the effectiveness of administrative costs of tax management by the method of conversion rate is based on the number of employees involved in the management of excise duties in the liner-controlled structure.
In the Czech Republic, the Customs Administration of the Czech Republic, which is an independent organizational component of the state and an entity.
In the Slovak Republic, the Finance Administration of the Slovak Republic ensures tax management, with customs authorities being an internal organisational unit, costs and revenue being included in the whole organisational unit.
Therefore, due to the possibility of comparing the efficiency of the management of excise duties in the calculation of the effectiveness of administrative costs, the costs and revenue of the Financial Administration of the Czech Republic were also included.
Administrative costs of the management of excise duties in the Czech Republic
The management of excise duties is a complex of administrative tasks performed mainly by the Customs Administration of the Czech Republic.
Some partial control functions are performed by other public authorities, but their importance is negligible.
In particular, the following departments shall be executed by the management of excise duties:
Directorate-General of Customs
department 23 tax

Unit 233-Tax checks methodically manage and coordinate the execution of the tax inspection agenda at customs offices;

separation of legal - decision-making activity in the case of non-tax law; activities related to proper and exceptional remedies; tax execution proceedings;
the branch of the customs office - decides on registration (except for the tax warehouse, entitled recipient for repeated acceptance, registered consignor), on the amount of security of the tax; prescribes and returns tax; exercises tax oversight and tax control; decides on security and forfeiture of goods;
customs office station - the exercise of tax oversight of the holding and movement of excise goods; ensures the performance of permanent tax oversight in the alcohol tax warehouse; decides on security and forfeiture of goods.
SR's financial management costs on excise duty management are constantly increasing, as with the exception of wage growth, investments for effective tax management and financial management electronization increase.
Although excise tax revenue grew, spending increased faster due to IT adjustments related to UNITAS project.
Salary expenses in SR are significantly influenced by the performance of permanent tax oversight in tax warehouses on alcohol, which the Czech Republic does not apply.
Expenditure of the Customs Administration of the Czech Republic on the management of excise duties increased significantly between 2012 and 2015 in 2015, this growth was mainly due to increased wage spending and technical support costs.
In the Czech Republic, excise tax revenue grew at approximately the same rate.
Wages in the Czech Republic are positively influenced by wider customs duties, e.g. weighing trucks, check on the fulfillment of myth duties.
The effectiveness of administrative costs in SR shows a slightly worsening trend year-round.
The number of employees did not change significantly, but the spending was growing per employee.
Also in the Czech Republic, the number of employees has not changed significantly, but the costs per employee compared to the SR grew slower.
Evaluation
In the Czech Republic and in SR, an important factor is the deteriorated effectiveness of administrative spending, which can be evaluated as natural developments.
In both countries, maintaining significant administrative demanding in the management of excise duties is a negative factor, confirming the non-decreasing number of employees in the field of excise duty management.
However, in SR, the management of excise duties with lower incomes is significantly more demanding for staff capacities.
Performance indicators for the management of excise duties
Excise tax management is a set of activities aimed at correct identifying, determining and securing the payment of tax.
The main processes in the management of excise duties are taxation, permissions and registration for activity, transport oversight, inspection and search of tax entities.
The number of administrative tasks and managed entities are indicators of the tax manager's performance.
The relationship between the observed indicator and the number of tax administrators expresses the effectiveness of the tax manager's activity and defines the cost of a particular activity.
Authorisations and registration for activity are a fundamental prerequisite for the handling of selected products for commercial purposes and transport them under a tax exemption scheme.
The tax administrator is obliged to exercise a systematic administration with a focus on supervision of the legislation and conditions laid down by the tax administrator, for which adequate personnel resources must be allocated.
The observed indicator was the number of valid permits or registration for activity on 31. December of each year.
The number of permits or registrations issued is not identical to the number of tax entities.
Administrative actions are specific administrative acts in the matter.
The monitored administrative actions are the frequency of the most important tasks of the tax administrator (tax claim, transport administration in EMCS), or activities that are the sequence of actions completed by a report or decision.

Authorization and registration for activity in Czech Republic
Tax warehouse:
Production, processing, store, receive or dispatch selected products may be approved by the tax administrator to operate a tax warehouse.
If the tax warehouse operator has multiple warehouses, a permit shall be issued for each separately, including tax security.
Taxation is not required for distilleries under permanent tax supervision by the tax manager (i.e. the physical presence of an official and the provision of equipment with the closures of the tax manager).
In the Czech Republic, permanent tax supervision is not applied.
The operator of the tax warehouse also registers for tax under Section 125 of Law No. 280/2009 Coll.
Authorization to operate a tax warehouse is a condition for transport of selected products conditional exempted from the place of importation into a tax warehouse, a legitimate recipient in another Member State, to the place of export in another Member State or a consignee in another Member State (replaces the status of registered consignor under Article () of the registered consignor. Article 4 (4) of the Treaty (10) Council Directive 2008/118 / EC).
Tax warehouse statistics do not include permits to acquire electricity, natural gas and tax-free solid fuels, which are analogies of tax warehouse permits.
Growing brandy produces alcohol with a reduced 50 % tax rate (CZK 14 / hl ethanol) - fruit distillates for growers. It is not a tax warehouse and the Ministry of Agriculture issued a permit to operate.
Reduced tax rate can be applied to 30 liters of pure alcohol per household of grower intended for personal consumption during the production period (July-June).
The record of the growing burning, held by and made available by the tax administrators, must contain information about the grower, the basic raw material, the distillate issued, the origin of the fruit and the production of the distillate.
The authorised recipient for the repeated acceptance of selected products and the beneficiary for disposable acceptance of selected products is entitled, subject to the authorization of the tax administrator and the conditions laid down, to accept or recieve selected products in a conditional system transported from another Member State.
The beneficiary is not the operator of the tax warehouse and the selected products under the tax exemption regime must not be stored or dispatched.
The user of selected tax exempt products is a legal or natural person who receives and uses, or according to Section 52 a or Section 53 of Law No. 353/2003 Coll. sells selected tax exempt products to another user; users have the status of tax entities without the obligation to register for tax.
Only by means of a valid authorization can be accepted and used by selected tax exempt products, from the supplier specified in the authorization.
Based on the authorization, mineral oils exempted from the tax can be sold to another holder of a use permit or user entitled to use mineral oils without permission.
Without permission, tax exempt mineral oils can be sold in lawful cases, e.g.
waste oils of less than 10 liters per calendar year, if the user produced them or created them during their operation,
selected tax exempt mineral oils in a unit package of a content of not more than 20 liters, intended for purposes other than engine drive or heat production, while at the same time intended for sale to the final consumer.
The transport of selected tax exempt products with the exemption document.
The alcohol distributor in the consumer packaging is entitled to sell or otherwise transfer alcohol put into free tax circulation after compulsory registration with the tax manager.
Based on registration with the tax administrator and the conditions laid down, the raw tobacco stored for a purpose other than the production of tobacco products.
A person handling special mineral oils is entitled to acquire, sell or otherwise transfer special mineral oils which are bulk or placed in a package exceeding 220 litres, depending on registration with the tax administrator and the conditions laid down.
The fuel distributor is entitled to sell fuel in the Czech Republic, except for the sale of fuel from the gas station, based on the concession issued and registration of the tax administrator under specified conditions.
PHM transport must be accompanied by a tax document, sales document or transport document, or delivery plan and bottling tickets.
These documents may be replaced by electronic documents sent before the traffic starts by the tax manager.
The operator of the gas station is the owner of fuel sold at the gas station.
Gas stations are places where the sale or dispensing of PHM is normally allowed in a fuel tank based on the construction office's permission.
The Ministry of Industry and Trade records gas stations and their operators broken down by: registered - normal selling or dispensing of PHM usually into vehicle fuel tanks; with defined access - operating usually in different business areas (e.g. quarries, saws, agricultural farms, transport organizations, construction courts), the sale is made here for the other side limited on the basis of specific contractual relations; non-public - fuel dispensing points only for the operator s' own consumption.
The gas station is not a construction or installation in the form of an operating tank (e.g. on the chassis) when the fuel is issued only for its own use.
Operating tanks are not subject to tax administrator's permission and are not registered.
Buy, accept and sell liquefied petroleum gases put into free tax circulation for resale, natural and legal persons can under the permission of the tax manager.
Authorisations must be allowed even when they buy or obtain liquefied petroleum gases for their own consumption exceeding 20 tonnes per calendar year.
Administrative operations in Czech Republic
Tax check is a set of actions. The subject of the tax check is tax liability, the claim of the tax body or other circumstances relevant to the correct detection and determination of the tax related to one tax proceeding.
Tax check can be done together for more tax proceedings of one tax body.
Repeated tax check can only be done under law conditions and justification at the start of the inspection.
The tax inspection is carried out within the deadline for the determination of a tax of three years, with the deadline being extended by one year under the conditions laid down by law (e.g. submission of additional tax proceedings, initiation of criminal proceedings in connection with the tax in question) or is being built (lawsuit, international cooperation).
The deadline for determining the tax shall expire at the latest ten years after the deadline for filing a proper tax claim.
Tax administrators are not required to carry out tax checks on each tax entity.
The start of a tax check sets deadlines for the possibility of submitting additional tax returns or additional tax billing (Section 141 of Law No. 141 280/2009 Coll.) and reopens the deadline for determining the tax (Section 148 of Act No. 280/2009 Coll.).
Based on its result, the official power tax may be measured.
Local investigation is an individual time-bound act (one day) where the tax manager sought evidence and examines premises, goods, documents, records, means of transport and transport packaging for tax entities and other persons involved in tax administration outside the premises of the tax administrator (e.g. at the tax body, at the point of sale, on the road during transport).
The tax administrator is entitled to borrow documents and things, take samples or secure them.
Based on the result of the local investigation, tax cannot be measured independently, but the tax body can be called for submission of additional tax returns (Paragraph 145 (145) of the basic Regulation). Article 2 of Law No. 280/2009 Coll.).
Control of traffic data in EMCS is not a local investigation.
The order of control bands for alcohol marking can be submitted to the tax administrator to the local labelling point only by registered person obliged to sign alcohol and is performed via intelligent forms that are automatically imported into the application of the alcohol marker registry.
The tax administrator processes the order, evaluates the adequacy of the quantity of control bands ordered and orders production.
He does not oversee the production of control bands.
Production is provided by the State Prices Printer, a state enterprise.
The customer of the control belt takes over the control bands with the tax manager of the local marking place.
Ordering tobacco stickers for cigarettes, cigarillos, cigars and smoking tobacco performs the tax return function.
The value of the tobacco sticker corresponds to the amount of the tax liability, with the tobacco sticker obliged to pay their value within 60 days of the date of their removal from the tax manager.
The customer is obliged to calculate the value in the order corresponding to the amount of the tax liability of the ordered tobacco stickers.
This period shall apply only if the value of tobacco stickers is ensured.
Order of tobacco stickers shall be placed on a form established by the Ministry of Finance in writing or through a data box with the possibility of using intelligent forms.
The production of tobacco stickers is provided by the State Prices Printer, a state company.
The tax administrator, which is the Customs Office for the Central Bohemian Region (Kutna Hora territorial workplace), ensures the purchase and transport of tobacco stickers to the tax manager, who further distributes them and further checks their transport, storage and use with customers.
Tax claims include proper tax returns, additional and corrective tax returns, including orders of tobacco stickers filed by tax entities.
No tax return on customs declarations and the granting of refund claims on: mineral oils used for heat production, other petrol used in business activities other than for heat production or engine propulsion, mineral oils used for primary agricultural production I'm sorry.
The fines imposed include administrative proceedings in the case of dealing with the found infringements, which are a set of follow-up administrative actions. The international exchange of information on tax entities (ELO) within the meaning of Council Regulation (EU) No 389/2012 takes place in the form of: application for administrative cooperation, responses to the request for administrative cooperation, spontaneous information, event reports, inspection reports.
Transport under the tax exemption regime between the Czech Republic and the EU Member States - the Czech customs office is the tax administrator of the receiving or dispatching tax warehouse or the beneficiary.
Performance indicators in SR
Authorization and registration for activity in SR
Excise tax management in SR is mainly provided by customs offices and excise duty department of the Customs and tax FD SR, whose excise duty management procedure is governed by individual excise duty laws and tax rules.
These laws define not only the scope of the authorization for CÚ and FR SR for the management of excise duties, but also the rights and obligations of tax entities in connection with registration or payment of excise duty.
The largest annual increase in tax entities (by 234 %) was recorded in 2012 and 2013, due to an increase in tax warehouses licenses issued, an increase in the authorized recipient's registration for recruitment and registration of a large number of user companies.
Legislative has clarified the transport of some bulk mineral oils, as well as the notification requirement if transported freely or. in packaging with a content of more than 150 liters or. 230 liters and also extended the list of mineral oils under control and transport procedure with other goods, e.g. o anti-engine knocking products, oxidation inhibitors, bituminous inhibitors, viscosity improvement products, anti-corrosion products.
For lubricating oils, a compulsory indication of their kinematic viscosity was introduced.
Approaching the registration process for selected tax entities within the meaning of national legislation in SR is specified in the following parts of the document.
Tax warehouse operator
Under the national legislation of the SR when registering the operator of the tax warehouse within all excise duty items, the person who wants to operate the tax warehouse must also apply for registration and issuance of a permit for the operation of the tax warehouse.
The resulting decision in the registration process is the registration certificate for the relevant excise duty, which the tax warehouse operator acquires legal personality for all tax warehouses.
At the same time, CÚ will issue a permit to operate a tax warehouse, which authorizes the operator of the tax warehouse to manufacture, process, store, receive or dispatch selected products under the tax exemption scheme.
In case the tax warehouse operator has tax warehouses in several places, the tax manager will issue a separate permit for each tax warehouse to operate a tax warehouse.
Transportation of the subject matter under the suspension regime is monitored electronically via EMCS.
A unique reference code is generated for each transport, called.
ARC code under which you can monitor the transport on-line and therefore in real time.
If the operator of the tax warehouse is also a person entitled to distribute alcohol, he is required to notify by electronic means CÚ the commercial name of the packaging of alcohol, volume and volume concentration of alcohol in the consumer packaging and the barcode EAN for each new type of consumer packaging that is placed in free tax circulation, no later than the date of its introduction.
Registered sender
Registered consignor is a special type of tax entity that cannot be registered as a tax warehouse operator at the same time, even if he sends an excise duty subject to the excise duty regime after his release for free circulation.
Under the national legislation of the SR, when registered consignor for all excise duties, a person wishing to dispatch an object of excise duty under the suspension procedure after his release for the customs procedure ′′ free circulation ′′ must also apply for registration and issue of CÚ authorization to dispatch the subject matter of excise duty under this scheme.
CÚ issuing a certificate of registration for the relevant excise duty and at the same time issuing an authorization to dispatch an object of excise duty under the suspension exemption regime after its entry into the customs procedure ′′ free circulation ".
Grower's brandy
The basic act for the operation of growing brandy is to obtain permission to produce alcohol in a distillery plant from the Ministry of Agriculture and Rural Development.
However, the Ministry's authorization itself does not entitle the holder of the permit to operate a growing burner.
In order for a person to operate a growing branding machine, he must submit an application for registration and issuance of a certificate of registration of the operator of the growing plant.
CÚ shall issue a certificate of registration for the relevant excise duty, which also authorizes the producer of the growing brandy to produce alcohol in the growing brandy.
The purpose of growing brandy is to provide services to growers.
Growing brandy can't be a tax stock.
The legislator allows alcohol produced in the growing brandy to apply a reduced tax rate of 50 % on the basic tax rate, i.e. 540 € / hl a.
The reduced tax rate shall apply to alcohol produced in a growing breeder of not more than 43 l and. per grower and household for one production season in tax territory.
The production period lasts from 1. 7. of the current year to 30. of the following year.
The production period is not the same as the calendar year and therefore, within one calendar year, a reduced tax rate can be applied to the produced alcohol multiple times, because the alcohol is produced in two manufacturing periods.
This is the production of alcohol outside the tax exemption regime, which means in practice that the alcohol produced is in free tax circulation.
The grower will pay the growers not only excise tax and value added tax, but also the price for the services provided.
Growing moonshine will issue a removal certificate to the grower, which serves not only as proof of origin and method of acquisition of alcohol, but also of payment of excise duty.
Transport of alcohol thus produced is not subject to monitoring by the tax manager.
Importer of the consumer packaging
National legislation enables persons who intend to import a consumer packaging of alcohol or cigarettes from a third state and put it into free tax circulation in tax territory, to ask CÚ to be included in the registration of importers of consumer packaging.
The importer of the consumer packaging does not register for the relevant excise duty, but CÚ gives him a certificate of inclusion in the registration of importers of the consumer packaging.
This certificate authorizes the importer to import a consumer packaging of alcohol or a consumer packaging of cigarettes from the territory of a third state.
At the same time, before issuing the checks marks, they must provide a tax guarantee for the amount of alcohol or cigarettes it wants to put into free tax circulation.
The importer of the consumer packaging must introduce into free tax circulation only the packaging marked by the inspection mark.
Therefore, they must present to the customs office of export the number and identification number of the inspection marks exported to the territory of the third State.
On importation, the importer is required to confirm the number of inspection marks imported back from the territory of the third State by the customs office of importation.
The importer shall proceed with the import of the consumer packaging in the sense of customs legislation, where the amount of excise duty is also included in the customs debt.
In case of the release of the consumer packaging into free tax circulation, the compound tax guarantee will be refunded to the importer or it can be used to pay the customs debt.
The importer of the consumer packaging is not in stock.
If the importer of the consumer packaging of alcohol is also entitled to distribute alcohol, he is obliged to notify electronically oběhu the commercial name of the consumer packaging of alcohol, volume and volume concentration of alcohol in the alcohol consumer packaging and the barcode EAN for each new type of consumer packaging which he puts into free tax circulation, no later than the day of its introduction.
Salesman of consumer packaging alcohol in free tax circulation
Due to the monitoring of alcohol movement in free tax circulation and the elimination of tax evasion by the legislator, the new tax institute has introduced the consumer packaging of alcohol.
A person who wants to hold a licence for sale must ask CÚ for a licence and fulfil legal conditions (business licence for business; integrity in relation to intentional economic offences; has not been withdrawn for years of sale; not in liquidation not even in auditions).
Since it is a consumer packaging of alcohol in free tax circulation, no accompanying document is required when transporting these goods.
To demonstrate the way the consumer packaging is acquired, e.g. an invoice that also contains the number of the holder of the distribution authorization.
The holder of the authorization shall, for each establishment, register for the calendar month, the number of accepted pieces of consumer packaging of alcohol, the number of products issued, the quantity of alcohol in consumer packaging, the state of alcohol stocks in consumer packaging on the last day of the month, and the registration of manka or surplus in the number of alcohol received and issued I'm sorry.
The holder of the authorization is obliged to buy alcohol in the consumer packaging or otherwise collect only from the person entitled to distribute during the business.
Distributor of the consumer packaging alcohol
Due to monitoring alcohol movement in free tax circulation and eliminating tax evasion of the legislature, the new tax institute introduced a distributor of the consumer packaging of alcohol.
A person who intends to hold a distribution permit must ask CÚ to issue a distribution licence.
Applicant must meet legal conditions (business licence for business; storage area exceeds 200 m2); annual turnover from the sale of consumer packaging alcohol at least 100 000 € or paid basic property of at least 100 €; minimum number of 000 počet 10 employees; no arrears against the customs office; no arrears on compulsory levies; integrity in relation to intentional economic offences; not withdrawn for ten years; not in liquidation or bankruptcy).
Since it is a consumer packaging of alcohol in free tax circulation, no accompanying document is required when transporting these goods.
For example, it is sufficient to demonstrate how to acquire a consumer packaging of alcohol. an invoice that also contains the number of the holder of the distribution authorization.
The holder of the distribution authorization shall, for each establishment, register for the number of alcohol packages received, number of pieces of consumer packaging, quantity of alcohol issued, alcohol stocks in the consumer packaging on the last day of the month, and registration of manka or surplus in the number of accepted and issued consumers packaging of alcohol.
The holder of the distribution authorization is obliged to buy alcohol in the consumer packaging only from another person entitled to distribute.
The distributor shall inform the data for each calendar month electronically within the 25. th day of the following calendar month.
Fuel reseller
Due to monitoring of fuel in free tax circulation, as well as tax evasion elimination, a new type of tax entity has been introduced, namely the seller of fuel.
There is no special regulation on the gas station in SR territory.
That's why gas stations in the national SR legislation are employed as fuel sellers.
A person who wants to sell petrol, diesel or LPG for final consumption in the free taxation of petrol, diesel or LPG for final consumption in the course of a business activity in the tax territory, must ask CÚ for a sale permit before starting the sale and present a document showing that the storage facility is verified and equipped with an appropriate verified measuring device allowing the amount of mineral oil to be measured when receiving and dispensing and the tank must comply with technical standards.
If the tax warehouse operator is a tax warehouse operator, a licensed recipient or a registered consignor, CÚ shall also issue licences to registered persons for the sale of fuel.
The seller of propulsion is obliged, among other legal obligations, to keep the registration of purchased and sold petrol, diesel or LPG for the calendar month and is also required to inform oznámit of a new supplier (distributor) of fuel.
The seller of fuel is legally obliged to buy or otherwise collect fuel only from a distributor of fuel or from a registered person.
Since these are fuels in free tax circulation, the accompanying document is not required when transporting these goods.
However, when supplying fuel through auto-sanitary, the distributor prints the so-called seller when overdrafts are overdrafted. bottler from a measuring device built in the auto-store.
This document shall include, in addition to quantity, the date and time of delivery and the registration number of the car assigned by the traffic inspectorate.

The tax manager in the territory of the SR during the tax oversight of mineral oils records tax evasion related to the transport of this type of goods.
First of all, it is an effort to avoid road checks during transport, so carriers use side roads, circumvent the toll selection system due to more difficult monitoring of actual transports.
Transportation of mineral oils in rebuilt tankers with double day are also being carried out.
Many times illegal transportation is accompanied by a vehicle that carriers report possible mobile patrols to change the route and avoid road control.
Fuel mixing with light fuel oils or. waste oils.
Fuel Distributor
Due to monitoring of fuel in free tax circulation as well as to eliminate tax evasion, a new type of tax entity has been introduced, namely a distributor of fuel.
A person who intends to distribute petrol, diesel or LPG in the free circulation in the tax territory of a business activity shall apply to the customs office for distribution prior to distribution and present a document demonstrating that the storage facility is verified and equipped with appropriate verified measurements equipment as well as list of suppliers and customers.
Distributor of fuels is obliged, among other legal obligations, to keep records of purchased and sold petrol, diesel or LPG for a calendar month for each establishment.
The fuel distributor is legally obliged to buy or otherwise collect fuel only from a fuel distributor or from a registered person.
The fuel distributor can sell only to the fuel distributor, registered person or fuel consumer in tax territory.
However, when supplying fuel through the auto-ester, the distributor prints the propulsion agents or sellers during overdrafts. fuel consumer, so called. bottler from a measuring device built in the auto-store.
This document shall include, in addition to quantity, the date and time of delivery and the registration number of the car assigned by the traffic inspectorate.
Since these are free tax circulation propulsions, no accompanying document is required for the transport of these goods.

Fuel Consumer
Special status in national legislation is the consumer of fuel.
A person who purchases gasoline, diesel or LPG in free tax circulation and stores this mineral oil in a storage facility with a volume of 15 liters or more, shall notify the customs office of this fact no later than before first place in the storage facility.
The customs office shall include the fuel consumer in the registration.
In addition to legal facts, the address of the location of the storage facility is obliged to indicate.
In practice these are large transport companies, cooperatives, bus companies, road construction companies and other entities.
The storage device shall be verified and equipped with measuring devices enabling the amount of propulsion (stavor, specific bar) to be measured at the time of arrival and dispensing.
The tank must comply with technical standards.
The fuel consumer must buy fuels only from the fuel distributor or from a registered person.
Since these are free tax circulation propulsions, no accompanying document is required during transportation.
However, when supplying fuel via auto-stern, the distributor prints the so-called consumer when overdrafts are overdrafted. bottler from a measuring device built in the auto-store.
This document shall include, in addition to quantity information, the date and time of delivery and the registration number of the car assigned by the traffic inspectorate.
For example, it is enough to demonstrate the method of acquisition of fuel an invoice that also contains the number of the fuel distributor assigned by the tax manager.
The tax manager in the territory of the SR during the tax oversight of mineral oils records tax evasion related to the transport of this type of goods.
Small independent brewery
The operator of a small independent brewery is a person who produces beer in the business and meets legal conditions.
Subject to compliance with the conditions laid down by law, a small independent brewery can apply a reduced tax rate, i.e. 2,652 € per hl / percentage of actual alcohol content.
Annual beer production is limited to quantity up to 200 000 hl beer.
Since beer production is outside the tax exemption regime, transportation is not required because it is in free tax circulation.
A small independent brewery cannot be a tax stock.
In practice, they are small family businesses, which also operate restaurants or bars in which they offer beer of their own production for sale.
Administrative operations in SR
This subcap brings the tax supervision of excise tax management to selected tax entities within the meaning of national legislation in SR.
The largest annual increase in administrative operations (by 5,3 %) was recorded between 2012 and 2013, caused by more traffic in the EMCS system.
On the other hand, the biggest decrease was recorded annually in 2014, up to 4,3 % due to a smaller number of tax checks ended and a smaller number of tax returns filed.
The decrease was about legislative changes.
Tax checks
Through the execution of the daňové tax control, it detects or examines facts that are decisive for the correct determination of the tax.
Zaměstnanci staff shall be demonstrated during the exercise of tax inspection by a delegation to carry out a tax check, including, among other things, the purpose and subject matter of the control and extent of the taxation period controlled.
In practice, this means that the controlled taxation period can be one month, but also more taxation periods.
The scope of the taxation period controlled is determined by CÚ
Tax check starts with writing a tax check registration.
Převzetí receipt confirms the receipt.
The borrowed documents are required to return vrátit within 30 days of the end of the tax check.
The Zaměstnanec employee will draw up a protocol from the tax check.
If the tax check determines the difference in the sum paid by the inspected tax body, declared or claimed by the tax refund, CÚ together with the protocol to the controlled tax body, the shall also send a call for comments on the findings set out in the protocol.
The tax check is terminated on the date of delivery of the protocol.
The deadline for carrying out the tax check shall be no more than one year from the date of its start.
Tax checks on registered persons and selected registered persons shall be performed as necessary, but at least once before the date of the right to fix tax, which is 5 years.
FG SR issued an internal management act adjusting the above mentioned deadlines due to the uniform procedure of the tax manager in the territory of the SR.
Local inquiries
Local investigation is the activity of the tax administrator, where he sought evidence, examines and examines the facts needed for tax management purposes.
The místním employee will write a registration and give his copy to the tax agency about the local investigation.
During the operation of a local investigation, the zaměstnanec employee has the right to unlimited access to land, to operational buildings, to rooms and places including means of transport, transport packaging and to accounting documents.
Recognition of the quantity of alcohol produced shall be made in the form of a local investigation.
The facts found are the basis for the exercise of the tax check.
Also, in the case of local investigation, CÚ is entitled to take samples as well as to secure the matter.
FR SR issued an internal management act regulating the performance of tax oversight and local investigation for individual excise duty subjects to unification of the procedures of the tax administrator.
Permanent tax oversight in tax warehouses for alcohol
The Slovak Republic's accession to the European Union on 1. June 5. also made a change in the field of excise duty management.
The need for more efficient spending of state budget funds in the management of alcohol excise duty, improving the business environment in the area and introducing legislative tools for more effective repression of the grey economy in the area resulted in the adoption of new laws in connection with the management of excise taxes in 2004
One of the measures brought by the new legislative amendment was not only the transition of the tax administrator in the field of excise duty management from tax authorities to customs offices, but also the introduction of the need for the tax administrator's presence in the tax warehouse to alcohol.
In the territory of SR, national legislation taxatively defines that it is possible to accept, issue, manufacture or process alcohol in tax warehouse only in the presence of a zaměstnance employee.
This does not apply to a tax warehouse that receives, stores or sends alcohol only in the packaging of alcohol.
At the same time, CÚ is obliged to secure employees in tax storage so that income, dispensing, production or processing of alcohol is not limited.
The operator of the tax warehouse has an obligation to secure the conditions of the working environment for pro employees.
Based on a contract concluded with FŘ SR for the premises provided monthly, CÚ pays the tax warehouse operator the rental costs.
In the tax warehouse for the manufacture, processing or storage of alcohol, the manufacturing plant for storage of alcohol must be adapted so that at any time the quantity of alcohol produced, processed alcohol, stored alcohol, including stocks of alcohol and alcohol contained therein can be detected.
